## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Start([Start Template Rendering]) --> CheckKind{kind == CronJob?}
    CheckKind -->|Yes| SetAPIVersion[Set apiVersion]
    CheckKind -->|No| End([Skip Template])
    SetAPIVersion --> SetMetadata[Set Metadata]
    SetMetadata --> SetSchedule[Set schedule]
    SetSchedule --> CheckSuspend{suspend defined?}
    CheckSuspend -->|Yes| SetSuspend[Set suspend]
    CheckSuspend -->|No| CheckDeadline{startingDeadlineSeconds?}
    SetSuspend --> CheckDeadline
    CheckDeadline -->|Yes| SetDeadline[Set startingDeadlineSeconds]
    CheckDeadline -->|No| CheckSuccessHistory{successfulJobsHistoryLimit?}
    SetDeadline --> CheckSuccessHistory
    CheckSuccessHistory -->|Yes| SetSuccessHistory[Set successfulJobsHistoryLimit]
    CheckSuccessHistory -->|No| CheckFailHistory{failedJobsHistoryLimit?}
    SetSuccessHistory --> CheckFailHistory
    CheckFailHistory -->|Yes| SetFailHistory[Set failedJobsHistoryLimit]
    CheckFailHistory -->|No| CheckTimeZone{timeZone?}
    SetFailHistory --> CheckTimeZone
    CheckTimeZone -->|Yes| SetTimeZone[Set timeZone]
    CheckTimeZone -->|No| ConfigureJobTemplate[Configure jobTemplate]
    SetTimeZone --> ConfigureJobTemplate
    ConfigureJobTemplate --> CheckTTL{ttlSecondsAfterFinished?}
    CheckTTL -->|Yes| SetTTL[Set ttlSecondsAfterFinished]
    CheckTTL -->|No| SetPodMeta[Set Pod Metadata]
    SetTTL --> SetPodMeta
    SetPodMeta --> AddAnnotations[Add checksum annotation]
    AddAnnotations --> CheckPodAnnotations{podAnnotations?}
    CheckPodAnnotations -->|Yes| AddPodAnnotations[Add podAnnotations]
    CheckPodAnnotations -->|No| AddLabels[Add selectorLabels]
    AddPodAnnotations --> AddLabels
    AddLabels --> CheckPodLabels{podLabels?}
    CheckPodLabels -->|Yes| AddPodLabels[Add podLabels]
    CheckPodLabels -->|No| ConfigurePodSpec[Configure Pod Spec]
    AddPodLabels --> ConfigurePodSpec
    ConfigurePodSpec --> SetContainer[Configure Container]
    SetContainer --> SetVolumes[Configure Volumes]
    SetVolumes --> End
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class CronJob {
        +String apiVersion
        +String kind
        +Metadata metadata
        +CronJobSpec spec
    }
    class CronJobSpec {
        +String schedule
        +Boolean suspend
        +String concurrencyPolicy
        +Int startingDeadlineSeconds
        +Int successfulJobsHistoryLimit
        +Int failedJobsHistoryLimit
        +String timeZone
        +JobTemplate jobTemplate
    }
    class JobTemplate {
        +JobSpec spec
    }
    class JobSpec {
        +Int ttlSecondsAfterFinished
        +PodTemplate template
    }
    class PodTemplate {
        +Metadata metadata
        +PodSpec spec
    }
    class PodSpec {
        +Map nodeSelector
        +Affinity affinity
        +List topologySpreadConstraints
        +DNSConfig dnsConfig
        +List tolerations
        +String priorityClassName
        +String serviceAccountName
        +String restartPolicy
        +List imagePullSecrets
        +List containers
        +SecurityContext securityContext
        +List volumes
    }
    class Container {
        +String name
        +String image
        +String imagePullPolicy
        +List command
        +List args
        +Probe livenessProbe
        +Resources resources
        +SecurityContext securityContext
        +List volumeMounts
    }
    class Volume {
        +String name
        +ConfigMap configMap
    }
    CronJob --> CronJobSpec
    CronJobSpec --> JobTemplate
    JobTemplate --> JobSpec
    JobSpec --> PodTemplate
    PodTemplate --> PodSpec
    PodSpec --> Container
    PodSpec --> Volume
```
